First let me say, I am not using this as a concealer or coverup, I'm using this solely for makeup contouring. So I apply my moisturizer first to a clean face and then use a tiny bit of my concealer (NARS All Day Luminous Weightless Foundation) all over my face. I then just dab the color I wish to use in this palette, on my finger and dab it gently on to my face. Because I don't rub it in with my fingers and my face is already moisturized, it spreads nicely where I want it. I apply as much as needed and then rub a bit more moisturizer in my hands and gently dab/pat my hands on my face. I hate the look of chalky or caky skin so by doing it this way my face glows all day! I've gotten many compliments on my new makeup. I really think dabbing this stuff on is the key to having it look perfect! Will buy again, just wish I could buy the colors I use the most, since the others are a waste. But for the price you can't go wrong!
